

  2.1.2.1: When fulfilled, a promise: must not transition to any other state.
    √ already-fulfilled
    1) immediately-fulfilled
    2) eventually-fulfilled
    3) trying to fulfill then immediately reject
    4) trying to fulfill then reject, delayed
    5) trying to fulfill immediately then reject delayed

  2.1.3.1: When rejected, a promise: must not transition to any other state.
    √ already-rejected
    6) immediately-rejected
    7) eventually-rejected
    8) trying to reject then immediately fulfill
    9) trying to reject then fulfill, delayed
    10) trying to reject immediately then fulfill delayed

  2.2.1: Both `onFulfilled` and `onRejected` are optional arguments.
    2.2.1.1: If `onFulfilled` is not a function, it must be ignored.
      applied to a directly-rejected promise
        √ `onFulfilled` is `undefined`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `null`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `false`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `5`
        √ `onFulfilled` is an object
      applied to a promise rejected and then chained off of
        √ `onFulfilled` is `undefined`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `null`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `false`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `5`
        √ `onFulfilled` is an object
    2.2.1.2: If `onRejected` is not a function, it must be ignored.
      applied to a directly-fulfilled promise
        √ `onRejected` is `undefined`
        √ `onRejected` is `null`
        √ `onRejected` is `false`
        √ `onRejected` is `5`
        √ `onRejected` is an object
      applied to a promise fulfilled and then chained off of
        √ `onFulfilled` is `undefined`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `null`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `false`
        √ `onFulfilled` is `5`
        √ `onFulfilled` is an object

  2.2.2: If `onFulfilled` is a function,
    2.2.2.1: it must be called after `promise` is fulfilled, with `promise`’s fulfillment value as its first argument.
      √ already-fulfilled
      11) immediately-fulfilled
      12) eventually-fulfilled
    2.2.2.2: it must not be called before `promise` is fulfilled
      13) fulfilled after a delay
      14) never fulfilled
    2.2.2.3: it must not be called more than once.
      √ already-fulfilled
      15) trying to fulfill a pending promise more than once, immediately
      16) trying to fulfill a pending promise more than once, delayed
      17) trying to fulfill a pending promise more than once, immediately then delayed
      18) when multiple `then` calls are made, spaced apart in time
      19) when `then` is interleaved with fulfillment

  2.2.3: If `onRejected` is a function,
    2.2.3.1: it must be called after `promise` is rejected, with `promise`’s rejection reason as its first argument.
      √ already-rejected
      20) immediately-rejected
      21) eventually-rejected
    2.2.3.2: it must not be called before `promise` is rejected
      22) rejected after a delay
      23) never rejected
    2.2.3.3: it must not be called more than once.
      √ already-rejected
      24) trying to reject a pending promise more than once, immediately
      25) trying to reject a pending promise more than once, delayed
      26) trying to reject a pending promise more than once, immediately then delayed
      27) when multiple `then` calls are made, spaced apart in time
      28) when `then` is interleaved with rejection

  2.2.4: `onFulfilled` or `onRejected` must not be called until the execution context stack contains only platform code.
    `then` returns before the promise becomes fulfilled or rejected
      √ already-fulfilled
      29) immediately-fulfilled
      30) eventually-fulfilled
      √ already-rejected
      31) immediately-rejected
      32) eventually-rejected
    Clean-stack execution ordering tests (fulfillment case)
      33) when `onFulfilled` is added immediately before the promise is fulfilled
      34) when `onFulfilled` is added immediately after the promise is fulfilled
      √ when one `onFulfilled` is added inside another `onFulfilled`
      √ when `onFulfilled` is added inside an `onRejected`
      35) when the promise is fulfilled asynchronously
    Clean-stack execution ordering tests (rejection case)
      36) when `onRejected` is added immediately before the promise is rejected
      37) when `onRejected` is added immediately after the promise is rejected
      √ when `onRejected` is added inside an `onFulfilled`
      √ when one `onRejected` is added inside another `onRejected`
      38) when the promise is rejected asynchronously

  2.2.5 `onFulfilled` and `onRejected` must be called as functions (i.e. with no `this` value).
    strict mode
      √ fulfilled
      √ rejected
    sloppy mode
      √ fulfilled
      √ rejected

  2.2.6: `then` may be called multiple times on the same promise.
    2.2.6.1: If/when `promise` is fulfilled, all respective `onFulfilled` callbacks must execute in the order of their originating calls to `then`.
      multiple boring fulfillment handlers
        √ already-fulfilled
        39) immediately-fulfilled
        40) eventually-fulfilled
      multiple fulfillment handlers, one of which throws
        √ already-fulfilled
        41) immediately-fulfilled
        42) eventually-fulfilled
      results in multiple branching chains with their own fulfillment values
        √ already-fulfilled
        43) immediately-fulfilled
        44) eventually-fulfilled
      `onFulfilled` handlers are called in the original order
        √ already-fulfilled
        45) immediately-fulfilled
        46) eventually-fulfilled
        even when one handler is added inside another handler
          √ already-fulfilled
          47) immediately-fulfilled
          48) eventually-fulfilled
    2.2.6.2: If/when `promise` is rejected, all respective `onRejected` callbacks must execute in the order of their originating calls to `then`.
      multiple boring rejection handlers
        √ already-rejected
        49) immediately-rejected
        50) eventually-rejected
      multiple rejection handlers, one of which throws
        √ already-rejected
        51) immediately-rejected
        52) eventually-rejected
      results in multiple branching chains with their own fulfillment values
        √ already-rejected
        53) immediately-rejected
        54) eventually-rejected
      `onRejected` handlers are called in the original order
        √ already-rejected
        55) immediately-rejected
        56) eventually-rejected
        even when one handler is added inside another handler
          √ already-rejected
          57) immediately-rejected
          58) eventually-rejected

  2.2.7: `then` must return a promise: `promise2 = promise1.then(onFulfilled, onRejected)`

      `onFulfilled` is `undefined`

  2.3.1: If `promise` and `x` refer to the same object, reject `promise` with a `TypeError' as the reason.
    √ via return from a fulfilled promise
    √ via return from a rejected promise

  2.3.2: If `x` is a promise, adopt its state
    2.3.2.1: If `x` is pending, `promise` must remain pending until `x` is fulfilled or rejected.
      128) via return from a fulfilled promise
      129) via return from a rejected promise
    2.3.2.2: If/when `x` is fulfilled, fulfill `promise` with the same value.
      `x` is already-fulfilled
        √ via return from a fulfilled promise
        √ via return from a rejected promise
      `x` is eventually-fulfilled
        130) via return from a fulfilled promise
        131) via return from a rejected promise
    2.3.2.3: If/when `x` is rejected, reject `promise` with the same reason.
      `x` is already-rejected
        √ via return from a fulfilled promise
        √ via return from a rejected promise
      `x` is eventually-rejected
        132) via return from a fulfilled promise
        133) via return from a rejected promise

      2.3.3.3.2: If/when `rejectPromise` is called with reason `r`, reject `promise` with `r`
        `r` is `undefined`
          `then` calls `rejectPromise` synchronously
            √ via return from a fulfilled promise
            √ via return from a rejected promise
          `then` calls `rejectPromise` asynchronously
            √ via return from a fulfilled promise
            √ via return from a rejected promise
        `r` is `null`
          `then` calls `rejectPromise` synchronously
            √ via return from a fulfilled promise
            √ via return from a rejected promise
          `then` calls `rejectPromise` asynchronously
            √ via return from a fulfilled promise
            √ via return from a rejected promise
        `r` is `false`
